  Variable legend: `rho^(qm)` is the line state on the total carrier with boundary sectors.
  Reading: cycle completion / timed transmutation / circulation circuit line.
  Confidence: mixed

### Game Theory

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P_1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P_1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: root fixation / fluid carriage / extraction circuit line.
